***свистнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свистнуть.html>сви́стнуть</a> (8666)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свистнуть.html>сви́стнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svístnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свистеть.html>свисте́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to whistle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smack, to slap</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sneak, to pinch, to steal</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свита.html>свита</a> (7101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">świta</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Suite</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">suite</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свита.html>сви́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svíta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свита.html>сви́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свита.html>сви́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свита.html>свит</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>suite, escort, retinue, entourage</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> suite</li></ol>

***свить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свить.html>свить</a> (21294)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свить.html>свить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>вить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">свива́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wind</li>
<li>to twist, to weave
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свить.html>свить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:венок.html>вено́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svitʹ</b> venók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to weave a garland</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свить.html>свить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнездо.html>гнездо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svitʹ</b> gnezdó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to build / make a nests; <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to put down roots in some place, to settle down in some place</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свить.html>свить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:веревка.html>верёвки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> кого́-либо разг</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svitʹ</b> verjóvki iz kovó-libo razg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn / twist smb. round one's little finger</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go crazy</li>

***свобода.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́да</a> (796)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́да</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svoboda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*svoboda</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">freedom</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svobóda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́ды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́д</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>freedom, liberty
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:государство.html>госуда́рство</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́ды</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́да</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:государство.html>госуда́рства</a>. (влади́мир ле́нин)</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Poká jestʹ gosudárstvo, net <b>svobódy</b>. Kogdá búdet <b>svobóda</b>, ne búdet gosudárstva. (Vladímir Lénin)</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">While the State exists, there can be no <b>freedom</b>. When there is <b>freedom</b> there will be no State. (Vladimir Lenin)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свободный.html>свобо́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svobódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свободно.html>свобо́дно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svobódno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>freely <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">without interference or restriction</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>freely, easily <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">without difficulties</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свободно.html>свобо́дно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́т</a> по-ру́сски.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Svobódno govorít po-rússki.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He speaks Russian fluently.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свободный.html>свобо́дный</a> (5681)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́да</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svobóda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свободный.html>свобо́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svobódnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>free (not subject to limitations, not subject to rigid control)</li>
<li>free, unrestricted, free access</li>
<li>free, vacant, unoccupied, empty, spare</li>
<li>loose, spacious, loose-fitting</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> free, not bound to other elements, free valence.</li></ol>

***свод.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>свод</a> (6168)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъvodъ</i>. Synchronically analyzable as deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>свод</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svod</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>сво́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>сво́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>сво́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vault, arch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:небесный.html>небе́сный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>свод</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nebésnyj <b>svod</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">firmament, the vault of heaven</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребро.html>рёбра</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>сво́да</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rjóbra <b>svóda</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">fan tracery</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пята.html>пята́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>сво́да</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pjatá <b>svóda</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">abutment</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:образовывать.html>образо́вывать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>свод</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obrazóvyvatʹ <b>svod</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to roof, to overarch</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрывать.html>перекрыва́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>сво́дом</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">perekryvátʹ <b>svódom</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to arch</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крестовый.html>кресто́вый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>свод</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krestóvyj <b>svod</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">cross-vaulting, groined vault</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">стрельчатый <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>свод</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">strelʹčatyj <b>svod</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">ogive</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обратный.html>обра́тный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>свод</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obrátnyj <b>svod</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">invert</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>крыло́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>сво́да</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kryló <b>svóda</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">haunch</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возведение.html>возведе́ние</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>сво́да</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vozvedénije <b>svóda</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">vaulting</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возводить.html>возводи́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>свод</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vozvodítʹ <b>svod</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to vault</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пазуха.html>па́зуха</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>сво́да</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pázuxa <b>svóda</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">spandrel</span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круглый.html>кру́глый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>свод</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krúglyj <b>svod</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">calotte</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> code
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>свод</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́нов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svod</b> zakónov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">code of laws, legal code; statute book</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a> (4119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свести.html>свести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lead, to take <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from somewhere</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаз</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">glaz ne <b>svodítʹ</b> s kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not to take one's eyes off someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:могила.html>моги́лу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svodítʹ</b> kovó-libo v mogílu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring somebody to his grave</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ума́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svodítʹ</b> s umá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive crazy</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to lead from (one's) mind</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bring together, to throw together
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>концы́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>конца́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svodítʹ</b> koncý s koncámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make both ends meet</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to bring together ends with ends</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дружба.html>дру́жбу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svodítʹ</b> drúžbu s kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make friends with someone</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to bring together friendship with someone</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to reduce <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to bring <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:счет.html>счёты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svodítʹ</b> sčóty s kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to settle a score with someone, to square accounts with someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:разговор.html>разгово́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> что́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svodítʹ</b> razgovór na štó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lead the conversation to something</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>нулю́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svodítʹ</b> na net, <b>svodítʹ</b> k nuljú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring to nothing, to reduce to zero, to cancel, to invalidate</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шутка.html>шу́тке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svodítʹ</b> k šútke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn into a joke</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to remove</li>
<li>to trace <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">a picture</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сводиться.html>своди́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свестись.html>свести́сь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to boil down <i>(to)</i>, to come <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сводиться.html>сво́дится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нравственный.html>нра́вственному</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́су</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vsjó <b>svóditsja</b> k nrávstvennomu voprósu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">it boils down to a question of morality</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сводиться.html>сво́дится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>самому</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto <b>svóditsja</b> k tomú že samomu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">it comes to the same (thing)</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сводиться.html>своди́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>нулю́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svodítʹsja</b> k nuljú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to come to naught</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сводиться.html>своди́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svodítʹsja</b> na net</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to come to naught</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come off <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a transfer picture</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сводящийся.html>сводя́щийся</a> (7020)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сводящийся.html>сводя́щийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svodjáščijsja</span>)
</p>

***свозить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свозить.html>свози́ть</a> (16960)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свозить.html>свози́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svozítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свезти.html>свезти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to transport down, to drive down</li>
<li>to transport away, to carry away <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">by vehicle</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gather together</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свозить.html>свози́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svozítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to transport there and back, to drive there and back</li></ol>

***свой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a> (66)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*svojь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*swoyos</i>. Cognates include Latin suus, Ancient Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἕ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hé</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Sanskrit <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa"><b>स्व</b>तह्</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><b>sva</b>taḥ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and perhaps Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><b>se</b>lf</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svoj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive-possessive pronoun</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> one's own; my, his, her, its, our, your, their <i>(always refers to the subject of the sentence)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>курю́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сигара.html>сига́ру</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja kurjú <b>svojú</b> sigáru.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’m smoking my cigar.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>ку́рим</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сигара.html>сига́ры</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My kúrim <b>svoí</b> sigáry.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We’re smoking our cigars.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>ку́рит</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сигара.html>сига́ру</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On kúrit <b>svojú</b> sigáru.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He’s smoking his cigar (his own).</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>ку́рит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сигара.html>сига́ру</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On kúrit jevó sigáru.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He’s smoking his (the other guy’s) cigar.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>ку́рит</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сигара.html>сига́ру</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná kúrit <b>svojú</b> sigáru.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She’s smoking her cigar (her own).</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>ку́рит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сигара.html>сига́ру</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná kúrit jejó sigáru.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She’s smoking her (the other lady's) cigar.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>peculiar</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> riffraff, rabble</li>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свора.html>сво́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svóra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свора.html>сво́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свора.html>сво́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свора.html>сво́р</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pack (number of hounds or dogs)</li>
<li>gang</li></ol>
